Find your place in our partner ecosystem

Carbon accounting platforms

Helping businesses measure Scope 1, 2 and 3 emissions, as well as Product Life Cycle and Transaction analysis.

ESG platforms

Partners specializing in collecting data, measuring performance, and providing insights and reporting for stakeholders.

Technology & implementation

Specialist partners building climate action into apps, products and services using the Patch API.

Consulting & advisory

Helping businesses navigate the voluntary carbon market, and making informed decisions on including carbon removal efforts.

Carbon credit suppliers

Businesses that develop, finance, or otherwise help scale climate solutions, including nature-based approaches and human-engineered approaches.

Something else?

From financing climate projects, to measurement, reporting and verification, Patch collaborates with climate experts.

Why partner with Patch?
By partnering with Patch, you can reach a growing range of customers, deepen relationships, grow revenue and unlock new monetization opportunities.

“The Patch and Greenly partnership is powering climate action on a global scale, aligning our capabilities in measurement and reduction, with Patch integrated into our product to enable our clients to purchase vetted carbon credits. Our sales, account management, and marketing teams collaborate well, hosting webinars, creating reports and guides, and driving activations that help both businesses grow.”

Alexis Normand
CEO at Greenly

“It was refreshingly easy to leverage the Patch API to provide our customers with access to a portfolio of carbon credit projects. The clear product documentation, simple product integration steps, and the responsiveness of the Patch team enabled us to complete integration within a week.”

Annalee Bloomfield
CEO at Sustain.Life

"It has been a pleasure to work with Patch to grow our revenue and manage our carbon credit operations. They seamlessly connect us to new customers and support our transactions while partnering with us to build products that are critical to our growth.”

Rahul Shendure
CarbonBuilt CEO, Director

“Patch's Radius platform is helping to increase transparency in the voluntary carbon market. It is adding rigor to the carbon credit procurement process, as well as a seamless experience for any company to meet the Climate Neutral Certification Standard”

Ellie Read
Certification Director at Climate Neutral
